TITLE: Signicat Authentication API Reference
DESCRIPTION: API endpoints for managing authentication sessions with Signicat. Includes details on creating sessions and retrieving their status.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/email-otp/setup/authentication-api

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
POST /auth/rest/sessions
  Description: Creates a new authentication session.
  Request Body: (Not specified in detail, but implies session configuration)
  Response:
    201 Created:
      Content:
        application/json:
          schema:
            type: object
            properties:
              id: { type: string, description: Unique session identifier }
              accountId: { type: string, description: The account ID associated with the session }
              authenticationUrl: { type: string, description: URL to redirect the user for authentication }
              status: { type: string, description: Initial status of the session (e.g., CREATED) }
              callbackUrls: { type: object, description: URLs for success, abort, and error callbacks }
              allowedProviders: { type: array, items: { type: string }, description: List of allowed authentication providers }
              flow: { type: string, description: The authentication flow type (e.g., redirect) }
              language: { type: string, description: Language code for the authentication flow }
              requestedAttributes: { type: array, items: { type: string }, description: Attributes requested for the user }
              sessionLifetime: { type: integer, description: Session timeout in seconds }

GET /auth/rest/sessions/{id}
  Description: Retrieves the status of a specific authentication session.
  Parameters:
    id: { type: string, required: true, description: The unique identifier of the session to retrieve }
  Response:
    200 OK:
      Content:
        application/json:
          schema:
            type: object
            properties:
              id: { type: string, description: Unique session identifier }
              accountId: { type: string, description: The account ID associated with the session }
              authenticationUrl: { type: string, description: URL for authentication (may be updated) }
              status: { type: string, description: Current status of the session (e.g., SUCCESS, FAILED, ABORTED) }
              provider: { type: string, description: The provider used for authentication }
              language: { type: string, description: Language code used }
              subject: { type: object, description: Information about the authenticated user if status is SUCCESS }
              callbackUrls: { type: object, description: Callback URLs configured for the session }
              environment: { type: object, description: Environmental details like IP address and user agent }
              allowedProviders: { type: array, items: { type: string }, description: List of allowed authentication providers }
              flow: { type: string, description: The authentication flow type }
              requestedAttributes: { type: array, items: { type: string }, description: Attributes requested for the user }
              sessionLifetime: { type: integer, description: Session timeout in seconds }
  See Also:
    - [API Reference](https://developer.signicat.com/apis/eid-hub/#tag/Authentication-Session/operation/GetSession)
```

TITLE: API Reference for Get Process
DESCRIPTION: This entry refers to the API endpoint for retrieving the status and details of a verification process. It is crucial for understanding the 'failReason' field and other process-specific information.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/id-document-and-biometric-verification/provider-specific-integrations/onfido

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Processes API:

GET /processes/{processId}
  Retrieves the status and details of a specific verification process.
  Parameters:
    - processId (string, required): The unique identifier for the process.
  Responses:
    - 200 OK: Returns the process details, including status, provider, and failReason if applicable.
    - 404 Not Found: If the processId does not exist.
  Related Operations:
    - POST /processes: To initiate a new verification process.
    - GET /processes: To list all verification processes.
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: OIDC Authentication Flow
DESCRIPTION: Overview of the OIDC authentication process, involving requesting permissions, redirecting the user, and exchanging an authorization code for tokens.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/sbid/integration-guide/oidc-sbid

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
APIDOC:
  Flow: Authorization Code Grant
  Steps:
    1. Client requests authorization from the end-user by directing them to the authorization server.
       - Parameters: client_id, redirect_uri, scope, response_type="code", state (optional), code_challenge (for PKCE)
    2. End-user authenticates and grants permission.
    3. Authorization server redirects the end-user back to the client's redirect_uri with an authorization code.
       - Parameters: code, state (if provided)
    4. Client exchanges the authorization code for an access token and ID token by making a backend request to the token endpoint.
       - Endpoint: /token
       - Method: POST
       - Request Body: grant_type="authorization_code", code, redirect_uri, client_id, client_secret (if applicable), code_verifier (for PKCE)
       - Response: access_token, id_token, token_type, expires_in
    5. Client can use the access token to access protected resources or retrieve user info from the UserInfo endpoint.
       - Endpoint: /userinfo
       - Method: GET
       - Headers: Authorization: Bearer <access_token>
  Recommendations:
    - Use "Authorization Code flow" for most cases.
    - Always use Proof Key for Code Exchange (PKCE), especially for frontend flows.
```

LANGUAGE: APIDOC

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Transaction States
DESCRIPTION: Explains the different states a transaction can have, providing descriptions for each state including 'Invoiced', 'Started', 'Completed', 'Loaded', and 'Failed'.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/billing-and-analytics/transactions

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Transaction States:

- Invoiced: The transactions have been invoiced.
- Started: The transaction started, but did not finish with a successful response such as _Completed_.
  - Note: Cancelled transactions are included in the _Started_ state, as it is not a successful response.
- Completed: The transaction completed successfully.
  - Note: When a transaction is completed, the status changes from _Started_ to _Completed_.
- Loaded: The transaction initialised, but never progressed from its initial state.
  - Note: This state only applies if you have not migrated to our new platform.
- Failed: The transaction ended in an error state, due to an error occurring on our side.
```

TITLE: OIDC Scope Configuration
DESCRIPTION: Details on configuring allowed scopes for an OIDC client within the Signicat Dashboard's Access tab.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/sbid/integration-guide/oidc-sbid

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
APIDOC:
  Endpoint: /oidc-clients/{client_id}/scopes
  Method: PUT
  Description: Update the allowed scopes for an OIDC client.
  Parameters:
    client_id: string (The ID of the client)
  Request Body:
    allowed_scopes: array of strings (List of scopes, e.g., ["openid", "profile", "nin", "sbid-extra", "sbid-evidence", "idp-id"])
  Notes:
    - "openid" is mandatory.
    - Refer to the Attributes reference for scope details.
```

TITLE: Check DNS Status API (Domain Specific)
DESCRIPTION: Checks the DNS setup status for a specific domain identified by its ID. Returns 200 OK on success or 404 Not Found if the domain does not exist. Supports JSON and problem+json content types.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/domain-management

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
GET /domains/{domainId}/check-dns-setup
https://api.signicat.com/domain-management/domains/{domainId}/check-dns-setup

Path Parameters:
- domainId (string, required): The unique identifier of the domain.

Responses:
- 200 OK: Returns the DNS status information.
  Content Type: application/json
  {
    "records": [
      {
        "domain": "string",
        "type": "string",
        "value": "string",
        "valid": true,
        "dnsCorrect": true,
        "dnsValidationOverride": true,
        "partnerWildcardDns": true,
        "pointsToSignicatIdentityBrokerCname": true
      }
    ],
    "valid": true
  }
- 404 Not Found: Indicates the domain was not found.
```

TITLE: Start Step-up Session (POST /reuseid/id-stepups)
DESCRIPTION: Initiates a step-up authentication session. Requires user and device IDs, with optional eidProviderOptions to specify document types. Returns transaction details upon successful initiation.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/reuseid

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
POST /reuseid/id-stepups
https://api.signicat.com/reuseid/id-stepups

Request Body schema: application/json
userId (string, required): The ID of the user that will carry out the operation, in a valid UUID format.
deviceId (string, required): The ID of the end-user's device that will be used for the operation.
eidProviderOptions (object, optional): An object that contains parameters for deciding what kind of documents can be used, and which document should be the default.
  - docType (integer): If only one specific document is to be used.
  - docTypes (array of integers): If multiple documents are to be available. Recommend providing a defaultId when using multiple docTypes.
  - defaultId (integer): The first option shown to the user.

Responses:
200: Successful response
403: Forbidden
422: Unprocessable Entity (WebDAV)

Request samples:
Payload (application/json):
{
  "userId": "0eb66632-88d0-4ef4-8126-495c64a0abd2",
  "deviceId": "f8d74181-9e00-41ba-ba4f-43aa6a3dfea5",
  "eidProviderOptions": {
    "docType": 138,
    "docTypes": [
      138
    ],
    "defaultId": 138
  }
}

Response samples (application/json):
{
  "data": {
    "status": "Pending",
    "transactionId": "0160e8b9-dabc-4a16-b995-29d88e6f102f",
    "userId": "0eb66632-88d0-4ef4-8126-495c64a0abd2",
    "deviceId": "f8d74181-9e00-41ba-ba4f-43aa6a3dfea5",
    "dossierId": "e73801d2-3e7f-4184-8fda-67cc3b03416d",
    "processId": "0dca14cf-957d-46d9-b374-520f9c650859"
  }
}
```

TITLE: OIDC Client Configuration
DESCRIPTION: Steps to register and configure an OIDC client in the Signicat Dashboard, including setting the primary grant type and redirect URI.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/sbid/integration-guide/oidc-sbid

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
APIDOC:
  Endpoint: /oidc-clients
  Method: POST
  Description: Register a new OIDC client.
  Request Body:
    name: string (Name for the client)
    primary_grant_type: string (e.g., "Authorization Code")
    redirect_uris: array of strings (URLs for redirection after authentication)
  Response:
    client_id: string (Unique identifier for the client)

APIDOC:
  Endpoint: /oidc-clients/{client_id}
  Method: PUT
  Description: Update an existing OIDC client configuration.
  Parameters:
    client_id: string (The ID of the client to update)
  Request Body:
    primary_grant_type: string (Optional, update the grant type)
    redirect_uris: array of strings (Optional, update redirect URIs)

APIDOC:
  Endpoint: /oidc-clients/{client_id}/secrets
  Method: POST
  Description: Add a client secret for an OIDC client.
  Parameters:
    client_id: string (The ID of the client)
  Request Body:
    name: string (Name for the client secret)
  Response:
    client_secret: string (The generated client secret, to be stored securely)
```

TITLE: Signicat API: Create Process with Onfido
DESCRIPTION: This API documentation covers the 'Create process' endpoint for initiating an identity verification with the Onfido provider. It details the request body structure, including process type, document type, and essential process parameters like location.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/id-document-and-biometric-verification/provider-specific-integrations/onfido

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
POST /processes

Request Body:
{
  "provider": "onfido",
  "processType": "documentSelfie",
  "documentType": "passport",
  "processParameters": {
    "location": {
      "countryOfResidence": "NLD"
    }
  }
}

Parameters:
- provider: (string) Specifies the verification provider, set to "onfido".
- processType: (string) The type of verification process, e.g., "documentSelfie".
- documentType: (string) The type of document to be verified, e.g., "passport".
- processParameters: (object) Contains parameters specific to the verification process.
  - location: (object) End-user's location information.
    - countryOfResidence: (string) The end-user's country of residence (e.g., "NLD"). Recommended for accuracy.
    - ipAddress: (string) The end-user's IP address. Can be used as an alternative to countryOfResidence, but less reliable for country inference.

Returns:
- processId: (string) The unique identifier for the created verification process.

Related Endpoints:
- POST /dossiers: To create a dossier before creating a process.
- POST /processes/{processId}/start: To start the verification process after creation.
```

TITLE: Signicat DEM API: Get Record by ID
DESCRIPTION: Retrieves a specific record by its ID using a GET request. The ID must be a valid UUID. The response includes the full record entity, with different status codes for success and various error conditions.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/digital-evidence-management

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
GET /records/{id}

Retrieves a specific record by its ID.

Path Parameters:
  id (string, required): Unique identifier for a record. Must conform to the UUID/GUID standard.
    Example: 123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-556642440000

Responses:
  200 OK: Successful operation. Returns the full record entity.
  400 Bad Request: Invalid input. The response will inform you of which parameters are invalid.
  401 Unauthorized: Unauthorized. Valid authentication not found.
  403 Forbidden: Forbidden.
  404 Not Found: Record not found.

Server URL:
  https://api.signicat.com/dem/records/{id}

Example Usage:
  curl -X GET \
    'https://api.signicat.com/dem/records/123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-556642440000' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN'
```

TITLE: Set up API Client for Headless Authentication
DESCRIPTION: Instructions for setting up the API client to enable headless authentication for Swedish BankID. This involves configuring the necessary credentials and endpoints.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/sbid/integration-guide/auth-rest-api/headless

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
API Client Setup:
  Purpose: Configure the API client for headless authentication.
  Steps:
    1. Obtain API credentials (Client ID, Client Secret) from the Signicat Dashboard.
    2. Configure the base URL for the Signicat API.
    3. Set up authentication headers with the obtained credentials.
  Dependencies: Signicat Dashboard access, API credentials.
  Inputs: Client ID, Client Secret.
  Outputs: Configured API client instance.
  Example:
    // Pseudocode for client setup
    const clientId = "YOUR_CLIENT_ID";
    const clientSecret = "YOUR_CLIENT_SECRET";
    const baseUrl = "https://api.signicat.com/v1";

    const apiClient = new SignicatApiClient(clientId, clientSecret, baseUrl);
    apiClient.authenticate();
```

TITLE: OpenID Connect Simulator Authorization Request
DESCRIPTION: An example of an OpenID Connect authorization request URL to test the Signicat Simulator. It includes common parameters like `client_id`, `response_type`, `redirect_uri`, `scope`, `state`, `code_challenge`, `code_challenge_method`, and the simulator-specific `acr_values`.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/eid-hub/e-ids/simulator

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
OpenID Connect Authorization Request:

URL:
https://<YOUR_SIGNICAT_DOMAIN>/auth/open/connect/authorize

Parameters:
- client_id: <OIDC_CLIENT_ID> (Your OIDC client identifier)
- response_type: <GRANT_TYPE_CODE> (e.g., 'code')
- redirect_uri: <REDIRECT_URI> (The URI to redirect to after authorization)
- scope: openid profile (Requested scopes)
- state: <STATE> (An opaque value used to maintain state between the request and callback)
- code_challenge: ABC123 (The challenge for Proof Key for Code Exchange)
- code_challenge_method: S256 (The method used to derive the code challenge)
- acr_values: idp:simulator (Specifies the Identity Provider for the simulator)
```

TITLE: Assure API - Processes
DESCRIPTION: API endpoints for managing identity verification processes. This includes starting a verification, retrieving the status and details of a process, and downloading the complete results as a zip file.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/id-document-and-biometric-verification/provider-specific-integrations/onfido

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
OpenAPI Specification for Assure API:

# Tag: Processes

## Operation: startVerification
POST /processes
  - Starts an identity verification process.
  - No parameters are necessary.
  - Returns: Details of the initiated verification process.

## Operation: getProcess
GET /processes/{processId}
  - Retrieves the full information about a specific verification process.
  - Parameters:
    - processId (path): The unique identifier of the process.
  - Returns: Comprehensive details of the process, including status and results.

## Operation: getZipFile
GET /processes/{processId}/zip
  - Downloads a zip file containing the packaged results of a verification process.
  - Parameters:
    - processId (path): The unique identifier of the process.
  - Returns: A zip file with all process-related data.

## Related Endpoints:
- Assure Events: For real-time notifications on process status changes.
- Onfido Results: For examples of final result statuses.
```

TITLE: Signicat ID Document and Biometric Verification API Endpoints
DESCRIPTION: Documentation for key API endpoints related to identity verification processes, including starting verification, uploading images, and retrieving images.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/id-document-and-biometric-verification/provider-specific-integrations/onfido

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Processes API:

startVerification:
  Description: Initiates the identity verification process.
  Endpoint: POST /processes/{id}/start
  Parameters:
    - None
  Returns:
    - Status of the verification process.
  Notes:
    - Will fail if user consent is not properly obtained.

setImages:
  Description: Uploads images captured during the identity verification.
  Endpoint: POST /processes/{id}/images
  Parameters:
    - images: A list of image objects, each with a type (e.g., FRONT, SELFIE, BACK, PORTRAIT) and base64 encoded image data.
  Returns:
    - Confirmation of image upload.
  Notes:
    - 'FRONT' and 'SELFIE' are standard. 'BACK' is for 2-sided documents. 'PORTRAIT' is not provided by Onfido.

getImages:
  Description: Retrieves the images uploaded for a specific process.
  Endpoint: GET /processes/{id}/images
  Parameters:
    - None
  Returns:
    - A list of uploaded image objects with their types.
```

TITLE: itsme® Integration with Authentication REST API
DESCRIPTION: This section provides guidance on integrating with itsme® using the Authentication REST API. It outlines the endpoints, request formats, and response handling for authentication purposes.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/itsme/integration

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Integration with Authentication REST API:
  Description: Details on integrating with itsme® via the Authentication REST API.
  Endpoints:
    - /authenticate (POST):
      - Initiates an authentication request.
      - Request Body:
        - client_id: Your application's identifier.
        - redirect_uri: The URI where the user is redirected after authentication.
        - scope: Defines the requested permissions.
        - state: An opaque value used to maintain state.
        - authentication_context: Specifies the authentication method and attributes required.
          - Example:
            {
              "type": "ID_PORTAL",
              "required_attributes": ["givenName", "familyName"]
            }
      - Response:
        - authentication_request_id: Unique identifier for the authentication request.
        - redirect_url: The URL to redirect the user to for authentication.
    - /authentication-requests/{id} (GET):
      - Retrieves the status of an authentication request.
      - Parameters:
        - id: The authentication_request_id.
      - Response:
        - status: The current status of the request (e.g., PENDING, SUCCESS, FAILED).
        - authentication_response: Contains details of the authentication if successful.
          - Example:
            {
              "type": "ID_PORTAL",
              "attributes": {
                "givenName": "John",
                "familyName": "Doe"
              }
            }
  Example Flow:
    1. Your application calls the /authenticate endpoint.
    2. You redirect the user to the provided redirect_url.
    3. The user completes the authentication via itsme®.
    4. You poll the /authentication-requests/{id} endpoint to get the result.
```

Path Parameters:
- dossierId (string, required): ID obtained from the "Create dossier" response.
- processId (string, required): ID obtained from the "Create process" response.

Responses:
200: Process information successfully retrieved.

TITLE: MitID App Switching Sequence
DESCRIPTION: Illustrates the backend communication flow for the MitID app switching feature, detailing the steps from initial request to final authentication result.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/mitid/integration-guide/app-switching

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
MitID App Switching Sequence:

1. Check MitID app installation on the device.
2. Request backend server to create a request URL.
3. Create URL for MitID authentication:
   - OpenID Connect: Standard OIDC authentication request URL.
   - Authentication REST API: Use `authenticationUrl` from session creation response.
4. App receives authentication URL.
5. Open URL in Chrome Custom Tabs (Android) or SFSafariViewController (iOS).
6. User enters user ID in MitID web interface.
7. MitID web interface displays button to launch MitID app.

MitID App Interaction:

1. User clicks launch button; MitID app launches.
2. User authenticates in MitID app (PIN/biometrics).
3. MitID app triggers launch of native app via app switch URL.
4. Native app handles bringing foreground WebView back.
5. MitID web interface continues authentication (e.g., CPR number).
6. Upon success, user is sent to result URL:
   - OpenID Connect: `redirect_uri`.
   - Authentication REST API: Callback URL specified during session creation.
7. Backend server retrieves and verifies authentication result.
8. Return final page for the end-user.
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Signicat API - Start Capture Flow
DESCRIPTION: Initiates an identity document verification flow using Signicat's services. This API abstracts provider SDKs, allowing direct integration with web views for end-user image capture. It requires dossier ID, provider details, SDK type, and a redirect URL.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/id-document-and-biometric-verification

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
POST /dossiers/{dossierId}/capture

Generated server url: https://api.signicat.com/assure/dossiers/{dossierId}/capture

Authorizations:
basicAuth

path Parameters:
dossierId (string, required): The ID obtained from the 'Create dossier' response body. Example: 37191afe-25b3-4c30-b42a-b0ab64aa1d64

Request Body schema (application/json, required):
providers (Array of objects, required): A list of providers for verification. Use only one provider per request.
  - provider (string): The provider name (e.g., 'onfido', 'signicatpaper').
  - processType (string): The type of verification process (e.g., 'documentSelfie').
sdk (string, required): Identifies which SDK to use. Enum: "native", "capture".
  - "native": Uses the provider's native SDK (default for 'eid', 'readid', 'onfido').
  - "capture": Uses Signicat's SDK (default for 'signicatpaper').
redirectUrl (string, required): The URL where the end-user is redirected after image upload.
requestDomain (string, optional): The domain visible to the end-user, must be configured on the account.
captureParameters (object, optional): Provider-specific process parameters.
eventTags (Array of strings, optional): Tags for events API.

Responses:
201: The URL artifact was successfully created. The end-user is sent to this URL to load the JS SDK for image capture.
400: Bad request syntax.
401: Invalid Bearer token provided in the Authorization header.
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Mint API v1 Endpoints
DESCRIPTION: Provides documentation for the Signicat Mint API (v1), including endpoints for managing flows and instances. This includes retrieving all flows, a specific flow by ID, executing a flow, retrieving instances by flow ID or all instances, retrieving an instance by ID, downloading instance files, resuming an instance, and approving an instance.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/mint

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Mint API (v1)

Download OpenAPI specification: [Download](https://api.signicat.com/mint/swagger/v1/swagger.json)

Flow:
  getGet all flows
    - Retrieves a list of all available flows.
  getGet a flow by ID
    - Retrieves a specific flow using its unique identifier.
    - Parameters:
      - flowId: The unique identifier of the flow.
  postExecute a flow
    - Initiates the execution of a specified flow.
    - Parameters:
      - flowId: The unique identifier of the flow to execute.

Instance:
  getGet all instances by flow ID
    - Retrieves all instances associated with a specific flow.
    - Parameters:
      - flowId: The unique identifier of the flow.
  getGet all instances
    - Retrieves a list of all instances across all flows.
  getGet instance by ID
    - Retrieves a specific instance using its unique identifier.
    - Parameters:
      - instanceId: The unique identifier of the instance.
  getDownload an instance file
    - Downloads a specific file associated with an instance.
    - Parameters:
      - instanceId: The unique identifier of the instance.
      - fileId: The unique identifier of the file to download.
  getDownload a zip file containing all the instance files
    - Downloads a ZIP archive containing all files for a given instance.
    - Parameters:
      - instanceId: The unique identifier of the instance.
  postResume a instance by ID
    - Resumes a paused or stopped instance.
    - Parameters:
      - instanceId: The unique identifier of the instance to resume.
  postApprove a instance by ID
    - Approves a specific instance.
    - Parameters:
      - instanceId: The unique identifier of the instance to approve.
```

TITLE: Authentication REST API Response Example
DESCRIPTION: This JSON object represents a successful response from the Signicat Authentication REST API, containing user and authentication details.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/nbid/attributes-reference

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
OpenAPI Specification:

paths:
  /authentication/response:
    get:
      summary: Example Authentication Response
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Successful authentication response
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                properties:
                  id: { type: string, description: Unique identifier for the authentication session }
                  accountId: { type: string, description: Identifier for the associated account }
                  authenticationUrl: { type: string, description: URL to initiate the authentication process }
                  status: { type: string, enum: [SUCCESS, PENDING, FAILED], description: Status of the authentication attempt }
                  provider: { type: string, description: The authentication provider used (e.g., 'nbid') }
                  subject: 
                    type: object
                    properties:
                      id: { type: string, description: Unique identifier for the subject }
                      idpId: { type: string, description: Identifier for the Identity Provider }
                      name: { type: string, description: Full name of the subject }
                      firstName: { type: string, description: First name of the subject }
                      lastName: { type: string, description: Last name of the subject }
                      nin: 
                        type: object
                        properties:
                          value: { type: string, description: National Identity Number }
                          issuingCountry: { type: string, description: Country issuing the national identity number }
                          type: { type: string, enum: [BIRTH, NATIONAL], description: Type of national identity number }
                      nbidAuthTime: { type: string, description: Timestamp of authentication with NBID (Unix epoch seconds) }
                      nbidUpdatedAt: { type: string, description: Timestamp of the last update for NBID data (Unix epoch milliseconds) }

Example Response:
{
  "id": "58126fb8-c5e2-...",
```

TITLE: Signicat MobileID Signature API Documentation
DESCRIPTION: Provides comprehensive documentation for the Signicat MobileID Signature API, including details on starting a signature operation, request/response schemas, and status checking.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/mobileid

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
OpenAPIModel:
  __description__: The MobileID signature API provides you with operations related to signing for MobileID.
  __base_url__: https://api.signicat.com/mobileid/core

  Signature:
    __description__: Operations related to signing for MobileID.
    
    Start signing:
      __description__: Initiates a signing on the end-user's device. The operation response is returned with an operation state (`state`) set to `PENDING`, as the end-user now has to complete the operation on their device. The operation response contains a transaction ID (`transactionId`) that will be used for subsequent operations, such as checking the status of the operation.
      __method__: POST
      __path__: /signatures
      __requestBody_contentType__: application/json
      __requestBody_schema__:
        type: object
        properties:
          userId:
            type: string
            description: The ID of the user (`userId`) that will carry out the operation, in a valid UUID format.
            required: true
          device:
            type: object
            description: An object that contains the properties of the device to be used for this operation.
            properties:
              id:
                type: string
                description: The ID of the device.
              name:
                type: string
                description: The name of the device.
          tags:
            type: array
            items:
              type: string
            description: Used to tag callback event to enable filtering.
          operationProperties:
            type: object
            description: An object that describes the properties used to carry out the operation.
            properties:
              sessionTimeout:
                type: string
                description: The session timeout in milliseconds.
              preOperationContext:
                type: object
                description: Contextual information for the pre-operation phase.
                properties:
                  title:
                    type: string
                    description: The title of the context.
                  content:
                    type: string
                    description: The content of the context.
                  mimeType:
                    type: string
                    description: The MIME type of the content.
      __responses__:
        '201':
          description: The request to start signing was successful.
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                properties:
                  transactionId:
                    type: string
                    description: The transaction ID for the operation.
                  accountId:
                    type: string
                    description: The account ID associated with the operation.
                  state:
                    type: string
                    description: The current state of the operation (e.g., PENDING).
                  operationProperties:
                    type: object
                    description: Properties related to the operation.
                    properties:
                      preOperationContext:
                        type: object
                        description: Contextual information for the pre-operation phase.
                        properties:
                          title:
                            type: string
                          content:
                            type: string
                          mimeType:
                            type: string
                      pushSent:
                        type: boolean
                      sessionExpiryTime:
                        type: string
                        format: date-time
                      sendPush:
                        type: boolean
                  created:
                    type: string
                    format: date-time
                    description: The timestamp when the operation was created.
                  device:
                    type: object
                    description: Information about the device used for the operation.
                    properties:
                      id:
                        type: string
                      name:
                        type: string
                      state:
                        type: string
                      lastOperationType:
                        type: string
                      created:
                        type: string
                        format: date-time
                      lastUsed:
                        type: string
                        format: date-time
                  user:
                    type: object
                    description: Information about the user performing the operation.
                    properties:
                      externalRef:
                        type: string
                      id:
                        type: string
                      created:
                        type: string
                        format: date-time
                      lastUsed:
                        type: string
                        format: date-time
                      state:
                        type: string
        '400':
          description: Bad request.
        '403':
          description: Forbidden. The user is not authorised to perform this operation.

    Get state of ongoing signing:
      __description__: Returns the signing response with an [operation state](https://developer.signicat.com/apis/mobileid/#section/Common-concepts/Operation-states) for a specified transaction ID (`transactionId`).
      __method__: GET
      __path__: /signatures/{transactionId}
      __parameters__:
        - name: transactionId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
          description: The ID of the transaction to retrieve the state for.
      __responses__:
        '200':
          description: The signing operation state.
        '400':
          description: Bad request.
        '403':
          description: Forbidden. The user is not authorised to perform this operation.
        '404':
          description: Not found. The transaction ID was not found.

```

TITLE: Signicat SAML 2.0 Metadata Configuration Fields
DESCRIPTION: This section outlines the fields required to generate a SAML 2.0 metadata file for Signicat's EID Hub. It details both standard and advanced configuration options, including required fields and their descriptions.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/eid-hub/saml-2-0/saml-metadata

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Standard Fields:
  Name*: Name of the connection.
  Application URL: URL of the service provider application.
  Metadata URL*: The web address where you host the metadata.
  Select a LoA contract*: Select the mapping between levels of assurance.

Advanced Fields:
  Want assertions signed: If ticked, assertions will be signed.
  Want root signed even if the assertions are also signed: We recommend to always sign the root. If your application cannot handle multiple signatures, you may opt to disable signing of the root when signing the assertions.
  Use a transient format for the NameID: Tick this box if you only want a transient NameID.
  Include the SAML Assertion of the IdentityProvider if available: If the eIDs that you use are SAML 2.0-based, you may opt to receive the original SAML 2.0 assertion of the eID.
  Encrypt assertion: If you want to receive an EncryptedAssertion instead of an Assertion for added security, select this option. Note that some eIDs require you to receive an EncryptedAssertion.
    Data Encryption Algorithm: The algorithm to use for data encryption. Default is <http://www.w3.org/2009/xmlenc11#aes128-gcm>.
    Key Encryption Algorithm: The algorithm to use for key encryption. Default is <http://www.w3.org/2009/xmlenc11#rsa-oaep>.
  Assertion consuming services*: At least one assertion consuming service must be configured. Provide a location URL and a binding type (REDIRECT, POST or ARTIFACT).
  Single logout services: Enter the location URL and binding type (REDIRECT, POST or ARTIFACT) of any applicable single logout services.
  Artifact resolution services: Enter the location URL, binding type and index of any applicable artifact resolution services.
  Attribute consuming services: Enter name, index, description (optional) and at least one attribute.
  Certificate*: Upload all relevant certificates for the connection (at least one).
  Client organisation: Enter organisation name, display name, and URL.
  Hosting party organisation: Provide organisation name, display name, and URL.
  Contact people: Provide details about the contact people in your organisation. In Type of contact person, specify whether they are part of support, a technical department, name, phone number, and more.
  Select attribute filter: Select an attribute filter to control which attributes you want to include, or exclude, from the response.
  Select default eID rule: Select which default eID rule to use.
```

TITLE: OIDC Authentication Flow
DESCRIPTION: Describes the general OIDC authentication flow where an application requests permissions, redirects the user for authentication, and exchanges an authorization code for tokens.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/ftn/integration-guide/oidc-ftn

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
APIDOC:
  Flow: Authorization Code Grant
  Steps:
    1. Client requests authorization from the Authorization Server by redirecting the user-agent to the Authorization Server's authorization endpoint.
       Parameters: client_id, redirect_uri, scope, response_type='code', state, code_challenge, code_challenge_method
    2. User authenticates with the Authorization Server and grants consent.
    3. Authorization Server redirects the user-agent back to the client's registered redirect_uri with an authorization code.
       Parameters: code, state
    4. Client exchanges the authorization code for an access token and an ID token at the Authorization Server's token endpoint.
       Parameters: grant_type='authorization_code', code, redirect_uri, client_id, client_secret (if applicable), code_verifier (if PKCE used)
    5. Authorization Server validates the code and returns tokens.
       Response: access_token, token_type, expires_in, refresh_token (optional), id_token
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Signicat SBID Headless Flow API Documentation
DESCRIPTION: This documentation covers the API endpoints and parameters for initiating and managing headless authentication flows with Signicat's SBID. It includes details on creating sessions for different flows (QR, APP_LAUNCH, PAYMENT_NIN, PHONE), handling user interactions, and polling for status updates.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/sbid/integration-guide/auth-rest-api/headless

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
APIDOC:
  CreateSession:
    Endpoint: POST /sessions
    Description: Creates a new authentication session.
    Parameters:
      - name: sbid_flow
        type: string
        description: The type of headless flow to initiate (e.g., 'QR', 'APP_LAUNCH', 'PAYMENT_NIN', 'PHONE').
        required: true
      - name: nin
        type: string
        description: The National Identity Number (NIN) for PAYMENT_NIN flow.
        required: false
    Responses:
      200 OK:
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              properties:
                idpData:
                  type: object
                  properties:
                    qrData:
                      type: string
                      description: Data for generating the QR code (for QR flow).
                    autoStartToken:
                      type: string
                      description: Token for launching the BankID app (for APP_LAUNCH flow).
                    sbidStatus:
                      type: string
                      description: The current status of the BankID transaction.
                status:
                  type: string
                  description: The overall status of the session (e.g., 'WAITING_FOR_USER', 'SUCCESS', 'ABORT', 'ERROR').
      500 Internal Server Error:
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              properties:
                error.code:
                  type: string
                  example: "idp:server-problem"
                description:
                  type: string
                  example: "Internal server error occurred while cancelling the session."

  PollingForStatus:
    Description: Poll the status of an ongoing session to track user interaction and transaction progress.
    Endpoint: GET /sessions/{sessionId}
    Parameters:
      - name: sessionId
        type: string
        description: The unique identifier of the session.
        required: true
    PollingInterval: 1-3 seconds
    StatusUpdates:
      - If status is 'WAITING_FOR_USER':
        - For QR flow:
          - If idpData.sbidStatus is 'OUTSTANDING_TRANSACTION' or 'NO_CLIENT', update QR code with new idpData.qrData.
          - For other idpData.sbidStatus values, refer to the Status table for display information.
        - For APP_LAUNCH flow:
          - If idpData.sbidStatus is 'OUTSTANDING_TRANSACTION' or 'NO_CLIENT', continue displaying the launch button and polling.
          - For other idpData.sbidStatus values, refer to the Status table for display information.
        - For PAYMENT_NIN flow:
          - Inform the user to open their BankID app and continue polling.
    FinalizationConditions:
      - The session is finalized when status is 'SUCCESS', 'ABORT', or 'ERROR'.
```

TITLE: Get Images from Process
DESCRIPTION: Retrieves images (front, back, selfie, portrait) from a verification process. Requires dossierId and processId. Supports JPG/PNG formats. Authentication via basicAuth.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/id-document-and-biometric-verification

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
GET /dossiers/{dossierId}/processes/{processId}/images

---

**Description:**
Use this service to return images from the process. The images were either uploaded to the process directly through the Set images endpoint or by using the provider’s SDK to capture and upload them.

**Supported Depiction Types:**
- `front`: Front image of the ID document.
- `back`: Back image of the ID document.
- `selfie`: Selfie image of the end-user.
- `portrait`: Portrait image extracted from the ID document (available only for some providers).

**Supported File Formats:** jpg/png.

**Authorizations:**
- `basicAuth`

**Path Parameters:**
- `dossierId` (string, required): The ID obtained from the "Create dossier" response body.
- `processId` (string, required): The ID obtained from the "Create process" response body.

**Query Parameters:**
- `depiction` (string, required): The type of image to be retrieved. Enum: "front", "back", "selfie", "portrait".
  - Note: `portrait` is only available for 'signicatvideoid' and 'readid' providers.

**Responses:**
- **200 OK:** The image was successfully retrieved.
- **400 Bad Request:** This provider and process type does not provide the requested image type.
- **401 Unauthorized:** The Bearer token provided in the Authorization header was not valid.
- **404 Not Found:** The dossier was not found or the image was not found.
- **409 Conflict:** Conflict found while processing the request.

**Server URL:**
`https://api.signicat.com/assure/dossiers/{dossierId}/processes/{processId}/images`

**Response Sample (400):**
```json
{
  "instance": "/assure/dossiers/",
  "method": "POST",
  "status": 400,
  "type": "base:client-problem",
  "title": "Malformed Authorization header.",
  "detail": "Please provide a valid Bearer authentication.",
  "traceId": "034fb8bbc5da31f4dd2cf66e70ef313c"
}
```
```

TITLE: Processes API Operations
DESCRIPTION: Covers operations for managing verification processes, including creation, starting verification, retrieving process information, managing images, failing processes, and downloading results.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/id-document-and-biometric-verification

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Processes API Operations:

  - postCreate process: Creates a new verification process.
  - getGet process: Retrieves information about a specific process.
  - postStart verification: Initiates a verification process.
  - delDelete process: Deletes a process.
  - getGet image: Retrieves an image associated with a process.
  - postSet images to the process: Adds images to a process.
  - postFail process: Marks a process as failed.
  - getGet list of processes: Retrieves a list of all processes.
  - getGet video: Retrieves a video associated with a process.
  - getGet processes' external id: Retrieves the external ID of a process.
  - getDownload full result: Downloads the full result of a process.
```

TITLE: Signicat SBID Additional Parameters
DESCRIPTION: This API documentation outlines the various `additionalParameters` available for controlling the user flow in Signicat's SBID integration. It details each parameter's purpose, accepted values, and any specific requirements or notes for its usage.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/sbid/integration-guide/auth-rest-api/redirect

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
APIDOC:
  Control the user flow (additionalParameters):
    sbid_initial_flow:
      Values: DETECT, APP_LAUNCH, REMOTE_FLOW
      Description: Controls which authentication flow should be presented first to the user. DETECT (default) automatically determines the flow based on device type. APP_LAUNCH launches the BankID app locally. REMOTE_FLOW presents the QR code flow.
    sbid_app_redirect:
      Values: "myapp://redirect" (example, must be allowlisted)
      Description: Specifies the app redirect URL, which must be pre-configured on the Dashboard.
    sbid_app_ios_redirect_mode:
      Values: default, no_redirect, detect_browser
      Description: Determines how users are redirected after successful authentication with the BankID app on iOS. 'default' uses the standard browser redirect. 'no_redirect' instructs the user to manually switch back. 'detect_browser' attempts to detect non-Safari browsers and instructs manual switching.
      Note: This can also be configured in the Dashboard.
    sbid_require_mrtd:
      Values: true or false
      Description: Enables the Extra control (MRTD) feature for normal authentication. Requires 'sbidMrtd' to be included in 'requestedAttribute'.
      Security Note: Validate that 'sbidMrtd' returns 'true' to prevent tampering.
    sbid_auth_type:
      Values: NORMAL, PHONE
      Description: Controls the type of flow for Swedish BankID. NORMAL initiates the standard authentication flow (further controlled by sbid_initial_flow). PHONE initiates the BankID in telephone calls flow.
      Phone Flow Requirements:
        - Must include 'sbid_phone_initiator'.
        - Phone must be enabled in Dashboard configuration.
        - 'nin' must be sent as prefilled input.
    sbid_phone_initiator:
      Values: USER, OPERATOR
      Description: Defines the default selected radio button in the first screen of the Phone flow. USER selects the 'User' option, OPERATOR selects the 'Operator' option.
    sbid_intention_text:
      Values: "VGVzdCBpbnRlbnRpb24gdGV4dAo=" (UTF8 Base64 encoded example)
      Description: Specifies the intention of the authentication. Must be UTF8 Base64 encoded.
      Requirements:
        - Max length of Base64 encoded string: 1500 characters.
    sbid_intention_text_format:
      Values: simpleMarkdownV1
      Description: Defines the format of the intention text as simpleMarkdownV1.
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: GetSession API Endpoint
DESCRIPTION: Details for the GetSession API endpoint used to poll for authentication session status and retrieve user information.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/sbid/integration-guide/auth-rest-api/redirect

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
GET /auth/rest/sessions/{id}

Description:
  Polls for information regarding the session and ongoing authentication.

Parameters:
  - id (path parameter): The unique identifier of the session. This ID is obtained from the response of the CreateSession request.

Request:
  No specific data needs to be provided in the request body for Swedish BankID.

Response:
  On successful completion, the response will contain user information and session status.
  Key fields in the response include:
    - id: The session ID.
    - accountId: The account identifier.
    - authenticationUrl: The URL for authentication.
    - status: The current status of the session (e.g., CREATED, SUCCESS, ABORT, ERROR).
    - provider: The identity provider used (e.g., sbid).
    - subject: An object containing authenticated user details (id, idpId, firstName, lastName, nin).
    - callbackUrls: URLs for success, abort, and error redirects.
    - allowedProviders: List of identity providers allowed for the session.
    - flow: The authentication flow type (e.g., redirect).
    - requestedAttributes: List of attributes requested during session creation.
    - sessionLifetime: The remaining lifetime of the session in seconds.

Status Overview:
  - CREATED: The user has not completed the authentication yet.
  - SUCCESS: The authentication is successful. Authentication result is present in the response.
  - ABORT: The session was cancelled by the end-user.
  - ERROR: Something went wrong during the session, or the session was not completed in time.

Usage:
  Send a GET request to the endpoint with the session ID in the URL path.
  Example:
    GET https://api.signicat.com/auth/rest/sessions/58126fb8-c5e2-...

What to do with the response:
  If the status is SUCCESS, extract user information from the 'subject' object and identify the provider from the 'provider' field.
```

TITLE: Signicat FTN REST API Authentication Flow
DESCRIPTION: This documentation block details the core authentication process for the Signicat FTN REST API. It covers obtaining client credentials, acquiring an access token, and the steps involved in the authentication flow, including creating a session and retrieving user information.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/ftn/integration-guide/rest-api-ftn

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
API Reference: Signicat FTN REST API

1. Get Client Credentials:
   - Obtain your client ID and client secret from the Signicat developer portal.
   - These credentials are used to authenticate your application with the Signicat API.

2. Obtain Access Token:
   - POST to the token endpoint with your client credentials.
   - Endpoint: /oauth/token
   - Request Body:
     {
       "grant_type": "client_credentials",
       "client_id": "YOUR_CLIENT_ID",
       "client_secret": "YOUR_CLIENT_SECRET"
     }
   - Response:
     {
       "access_token": "YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN",
       "token_type": "Bearer",
       "expires_in": 3600
     }

3. Implement Authentication Flow:
   a. Build Authentication Request (CreateSession):
      - POST to the session creation endpoint.
      - Endpoint: /v1/sessions
      - Request Body:
        {
          "request_id": "unique-request-id",
          "client_reference": "your-client-reference",
          "identity_provider": "SIGNICAT_EID_HUB",
          "authentication_request": {
            "request_type": "SIGN_DOCUMENT",
            "document_data": {
              "document_id": "your-document-id",
              "document_content": "base64-encoded-document-content"
            }
          }
        }
      - Response:
        {
          "session_id": "generated-session-id",
          "authentication_url": "url-for-user-authentication"
        }

   b. Obtain User Information (GetSession):
      - GET the session details using the session ID.
      - Endpoint: /v1/sessions/{session_id}
      - Response:
        {
          "session_id": "generated-session-id",
          "status": "COMPLETED",
          "user_information": {
            "name": "User Name",
            "email": "user@example.com"
          }
        }

Related Resources:
- Attributes reference: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/ftn/attributes-reference/
- Signicat Authentication REST API: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/eid-hub/authentication-api/
- Message level encryption (MLE): https://developer.signicat.com/docs/eid-hub/authentication-api/receive-encrypted-responses/
- API reference: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/eid-hub/
```

TITLE: MobileID Admin API - Accounts Operations
DESCRIPTION: Provides operations for managing MobileID accounts, including fetching and adding accounts. Requires API client setup and appropriate permissions.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/mobileid-admin

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
APIDOC:
  operationId: getAccount
  path: /mobileid/admin/accounts
  method: GET
  summary: Get MobileID account
  description: Returns the properties of a MobileID account. The account ID can be provided as a query parameter or will be fetched from the access token.
  parameters:
    - name: signicat-accountid
      in: query
      required: false
      description: The ID of the Signicat account. If not provided, it will be fetched from the access token.
      schema:
        type: string
        example: "a-sdge-abcdefghijk123456789"
    - name: statistics
      in: query
      required: false
      description: Control whether the statistics (`AccountStatistics`) is returned in the response object. Statistics are returned by default.
      schema:
        type: boolean
        default: true
        example: true
  responses:
    '200':
      description: Successfully fetched the MobileID account.
      content:
        application/json:
          schema:
            type: object
            properties:
              created: { type: string, format: date-time, example: "2023-09-06T06:47:20.000Z" }
              modified: { type: string, format: date-time, example: "2023-09-06T06:49:23.000Z" }
              organisationId: { type: string, example: "o-d-Abcdefgh1234JC4Cczm4" }
              id: { type: string, example: "a-sdge-abcdefghijk123456789" }
              name: { type: string, example: "Sample Account" }
              type: { type: string, example: "SANDBOX" }
              state: { type: string, example: "ENABLED" }
              sandboxProperties:
                type: object
                properties:
                  sandboxDeviceLimit: { type: string, example: "100" }
                  numberOfDevices: { type: string, example: "0" }
              statistics:
                type: object
                properties:
                  numberOfActiveDevices: { type: string, example: "0" }
                  numberOfActiveUsers: { type: string, example: "0" }
              configurations:
                type: array
                items:
                  type: object
                  properties:
                    description: { type: string, example: "Created by admin." }
                    default: { type: boolean, example: true }
                    accountId: { type: string, example: "a-sdge-abcdefghijk123456789" }
                    id: { type: string, example: "5ecbf73d-90bd-46a7-a58e-9ac56d229e3e" }
                    properties:
                      type: object
                      properties:
                        applicationId: { type: string, example: "a-sdge-abcdefghijk123456789" }
                        inactiveDeviceDeleteRetentionTime: { type: string, example: "365" }
                    additionalFeatures:
                      type: object
                      properties:
                        passportScanEnabled: { type: boolean, example: false }
    '403':
      description: Forbidden. The user is not authorised to perform this operation.
    '404':
      description: Not found. The server cannot find the requested resource.

  operationId: addAccount
  path: /mobileid/admin/accounts
  method: POST
  summary: Add MobileID account
  description: Fulfills the onboarding of your account to MobileID by adding an account to the MobileID service. This is a prerequisite for all other operations.
  authorizations: None
  notes: This operation is a part of the onboarding process.
```

TITLE: SAML 2.0 AuthnRequest Example
DESCRIPTION: A sample SAML 2.0 AuthnRequest used for authentication. It includes essential elements like the Issuer, Destination URL, and specifies the protocol binding and assertion consumer service index.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/email-otp/code-examples

LANGUAGE: xml
CODE:
```

TITLE: Signicat Swedish BankID Redirect Flow API Reference
DESCRIPTION: This section details the API endpoints and parameters required for implementing the redirect authentication flow with Swedish BankID through Signicat. It outlines the necessary steps for setting up an API client and initiating the authentication process.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/sbid/integration-guide/auth-rest-api/redirect

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
APIDOC:
  Endpoint: /auth/redirect
  Method: POST
  Description: Initiates the redirect authentication flow for Swedish BankID.
  Request Body:
    client_id: string (Required) - Your Signicat API client ID.
    redirect_uri: string (Required) - The URL to redirect the user back to after authentication.
    state: string (Optional) - A unique value to maintain state between the request and callback.
    scope: string (Optional) - Defines the access permissions requested.
    nonce: string (Optional) - A string used to associate a client session with an ID Token, and to mitigate replay attacks.
  Response:
    status: string - The status of the authentication request (e.g., 'pending', 'success', 'error').
    authentication_url: string - The URL the user needs to be redirected to.
    error_description: string (Optional) - Description of the error if status is 'error'.
```

TITLE: SAML 2.0 Metadata Exchange
DESCRIPTION: Describes the process of establishing connections in SAML 2.0 by exchanging metadata between the Service Provider (SP) and the Identity Provider (IdP). The metadata format must adhere to the SAML 2.0 OASIS specification.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/eid-hub/saml-2-0/saml-metadata

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
SAML 2.0 Metadata:
  Purpose: To establish connections between Service Provider (SP) and Identity Provider (IdP) by exchanging metadata.
  Specification: Must follow the SAML 2.0 OASIS specification (https://docs.oasis-open.org/security/saml/v2.0/saml-metadata-2.0-os.pdf).
  Exchange Process: Involves sharing or uploading metadata in the Signicat Dashboard for trust establishment.
  Content: Describes the type and format of SAML 2.0 requests and responses.
```

TITLE: Get MobileID Geofencing Settings
DESCRIPTION: Retrieves the geofencing configuration for a specified device, including allowed continents, allowed countries, and denied countries.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/mobileid

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
APIDOC:
  Operation: GET /devices/{deviceId}/geofencing
  URL: https://api.signicat.com/mobileid/core/devices/{deviceId}/geofencing
  Description: Retrieves geofencing configuration for a given device.
  Path Parameters:
    deviceId (string, required): The ID of the user's device.
  Query Parameters:
    userId (string, required): The ID of the user performing the operation.
  Responses:
    200: Successfully fetched the geofencing settings.
    400: The user ID parameter is missing.
    403: Forbidden. The user is not authorized.
    409: The device is deleted.
  Response Sample (200):
    {
      "mode": "OPTIONAL",
      "allowedContinents": "EU",
      "allowedCountries": "CT",
      "deniedCountries": "RU"
    }
```

TITLE: OIDC vs SAML 2.0 Protocol Comparison
DESCRIPTION: Comparison of OIDC and SAML 2.0 protocols for authentication. OIDC is recommended for its industry standard compliance and simplified user session management compared to SAML 2.0.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/digid/integration/setup

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Protocol Comparison:
  - OIDC (OpenID Connect):
    - Recommendation: Recommended over SAML 2.0.
    - Features: Industry standard, simplifies user session management.
  - SAML 2.0:
    - Complexity: More complex to implement.
    - Requirement: Usually requires an existing federation agent.
```

TITLE: Signicat OIDC Authorization Endpoint
DESCRIPTION: Documentation for the Signicat OIDC authorization endpoint, detailing the base URL and the various query parameters required for initiating an authentication flow. This includes client identification, grant types, requested permissions, authentication behavior control, and redirection URIs.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/identity-methods/ftn/integration-guide/oidc-ftn

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
OpenID Connect Authorization Endpoint:
  Base URL: https://<YOUR_SIGNICAT_DOMAIN>/auth/open/connect/authorize

  Query Parameters:
    client_id: The client ID of your OIDC application.
    response_type: Specifies the required grant type for the OIDC flow (e.g., 'code').
    scope: A space-separated list of permissions requested by the application.
    prompt: Controls the behavior of the authentication flow (e.g., 'login' for forcing re-authentication).
    acr_values: (Optional) A space-separated list of key-value pairs to customize the authentication flow. Examples:
      - idp:ftn: Pre-selects FTN as the identity provider.
      - ftn_idp:<provider_id>: Directly directs the user to a specific FTN identity provider (e.g., ftn_idp:fi-op).
    redirect_uri: The URI where the user is redirected after successful authentication. Must be an absolute URI using HTTPS.

  Related Specifications:
    - OIDC Specification: https://openid.net/specs/openid-connect-core-1_0.html#AuthRequest
    - Signicat Dashboard OIDC Client Configuration: https://dashboard.signicat.com/oidc-clients/

```

TITLE: Get Person Information

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/apis/ongoing-monitoring

LANGUAGE: APIDOC

```
GET /monitors/{monitorId}/persons/{referenceKey}
https://api.signicat.com/info/monitor/person/monitors/{monitorId}/persons/{referenceKey}

Path Parameters:
- monitorId (string, required): The monitor ID.
- referenceKey (string, required): The person's reference key.

Responses:
- 200: The person was found. Response body contains person details.
- 404: Monitor or person doesn't exist.

{
  "fullName": "Hedda Hansen",

  "lastName": "Hansen",

  "nationality": "NO",
  "address": {
    "address": "Kirkegata 177",
    "zipCode": "3674",
    "city": "NOTODDEN",
    "country": "NO"
  },
  "screening": {
    "listType": "PEP",
    "source": "PEP_Edge"
  }
}
```

TITLE: Get Well-Known Configuration Utility (.NET)
DESCRIPTION: A utility method to retrieve and parse the OpenID Connect well-known configuration document. It caches the configuration to avoid repeated network requests.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/eid-hub/oidc/code-examples/signed-and-encrypted-tokens

LANGUAGE: csharp
CODE:
```
privateasyncTask<JObject>GetWellknown()
{
if(_wellknown ==null)
{
string metadata =await _client.GetStringAsync(Properties.Settings.Default.DiscoveryEndpoint);
        _wellknown = JObject.Parse(metadata);
}
return _wellknown;
}
```

TITLE: Onfido Native JS SDK Configuration
DESCRIPTION: Configuration details for the Onfido native JavaScript SDK when used within the 'Start Capture flow'. This allows customization of the workflow and user interface, specifically when the SDK is set to 'native' and the provider is 'onfido'.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/id-document-and-biometric-verification/provider-specific-integrations/onfido

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
API Reference for Capture Configuration:

## Endpoint: setConfiguration (Create Capture)
POST /capture
  - Configures the capture flow.
  - Request Body:
    - sdk (string): Specifies the SDK to use (e.g., 'native').
    - provider (string): Specifies the provider (e.g., 'onfido').
    - onfidoConfig (object): Specific configuration for Onfido native SDK.
      - workflow (string): Defines the user workflow.
      - ui (object): Configuration for the graphical user interface.

## Endpoint: updateConfiguration (Update Capture Configuration)
PUT /capture/{captureId}
  - Updates an existing capture configuration.
  - Parameters:
    - captureId (path): The unique identifier of the capture configuration.
  - Request Body:
    - Similar structure to setConfiguration, allowing modification of workflow and UI.

## Notes:
- The `onfidoConfig` object is crucial for tailoring the Onfido native SDK experience.
- Refer to the API Reference for detailed schema of `onfidoConfig` and its properties.
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Signicat API Error Responses
DESCRIPTION: Provides examples of common error responses from the Signicat API, including generic errors and detailed validation errors with specific parameter feedback.

SOURCE: https://developer.signicat.com/docs/error-codes

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Generic Error Response:
  type: string (URL pointing to error documentation)
  title: string (A short, human-readable summary of the error)
  detail: string (A more detailed explanation of the error)
  code: string (An application-specific error code

Example:
{
  "type": "https://developer.signicat.com/docs/error-codes/",
  "title": "Invalid authentication token.",
  "detail": "The authentication token provided is invalid. This may be due to an incorrect signature, expiration, or insufficient permissions.",
  "code": "invalid_token"
}

Validation Error Response:
  type: string (URL pointing to error documentation)
  title: string (A short, human-readable summary of the error)
  code: string (An application-specific error code)
  status: integer (The HTTP status code)
  traceId: string (A unique identifier for tracing the request)
  detail: string (A general message indicating validation failure)
  invalidParams: array of objects
    - name: string (The name of the invalid parameter)
    - reason: string (The reason why the parameter is invalid)

Example:
{
  "type": "https://api.signicat.com/mobileid/core/openapi.json",
  "title": "Invalid request parameter",
  "code": "invalid_request_parameter",
  "status": 400,
  "traceId": "4bf239c088089f2bca77d3a413909f1d",
  "detail": "Your request body parameters have failed validation.",
  "invalidParams": [
    {
      "name": "userId",
      "reason": "userId cannot be null or empty"
    },
    {
      "name": "deviceId",
      "reason": "deviceId cannot be null or empty"
    }
  ]
}
```
